<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:амбар.html>амба́р</a> (10483)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt"><a href = vnd.unilang:амбар.html>амба́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ambar</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) from Persian <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">انبار</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ambâr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амбар.html>амба́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ambár</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амбар.html>амба́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амбар.html>амба́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амбар.html>амба́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>barn, granary, warehouse, storehouse</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:амбарный.html>амба́рный</a> (22698)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амбар.html>амба́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ambár</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амбарный.html>амба́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ambárnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> granary, barn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:амбарный.html>амба́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:моль.html>моль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ambárnaja</b> molʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_grain_moth" class="extiw" title="w:European grain moth">European grain moth</a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Nemapogon_granella" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Nemapogon granella"><i>Nemapogon granella</i></a></span>)</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>granary</b> moth</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">амба́рище</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ambárišče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">амба́рщик</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ambárščik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***амбициозный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:амбициозный.html>амбицио́зный</a> (28733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амбициозный.html>амбицио́зный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ambicióznyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>self-conceited, proud, vain, arrogant, pretentious, showy</li>
<li>ambitious, aspiring, emulous</li></ol>

***американец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:американец.html>америка́нец</a> (2185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американец.html>америка́нец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">amerikánec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американец.html>америка́нца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американец.html>америка́нцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американец.html>америка́нцев</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американка.html>америка́нка</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>male American <i>(citizen, resident)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">американ(ец)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">amerikan(ec)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американка.html>америка́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">amerikánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американка.html>америка́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американка.html>америка́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американка.html>америка́нок</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американец.html>америка́нец</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>American woman <i>(female citizen, resident)</i></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американка.html>америка́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">amerikánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американка.html>америка́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американка.html>америка́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:американка.html>америка́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> sort of high-wheeled sulky, first presented in Russia in 1889 by American sportsmen</li>
<li>free pyramid (American pyramid), a variant of billiards</li>
<li>a sort of jobbing press</li></ol>

***аминь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аминь.html>ами́нь</a> (18193)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">аминъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aminŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Koine_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Koine Greek">Koine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀμήν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">amḗn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Biblical_Hebrew" class="extiw" title="w:Biblical Hebrew">Biblical Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">אמן</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">amén</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">certainly, truly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">آمين</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ʾāmīn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syriac_language" class="extiw" title="w:Syriac language">Classical Syriac</a></span> <i class="Syrc mention" lang="syc">ܐܡܝܢ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="syc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">'āmēn</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:амнистия.html>амни́стия</a> (14350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From obsolete <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">amnistja</i> (now <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">amnestia</i>).

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амнистия.html>амни́стия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">amnístija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амнистия.html>амни́стии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амнистия.html>амни́стии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амнистия.html>амни́стий</a></b>)

***аморальный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аморальный.html>амора́льный</a> (22173)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Most likely based on either <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">amoral</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">amoral(isch)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The latter has both meanings "immoral" and "amoral".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аморальный.html>амора́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">amorálʹnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)амора́льнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)амора́льней</b>)
</p>

<li>immoral</li></ol>

***амортизатор.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:амортизатор.html>амортиза́тор</a> (13669)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амортизатор.html>амортиза́тор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">amortizátor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амортизатор.html>амортиза́тора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амортизатор.html>амортиза́торы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амортизатор.html>амортиза́торов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">device to absorb shocks</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> shock absorber, cushion, dashpot</li></ol>

***ампутированный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ампутировать.html>ампути́рованный</a> (28806)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ампутировать.html>ампути́рованный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">amputírovannyj</span>)
</p>

***амур.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:амур.html>аму́р</a> (12944)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">amour</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амур.html>аму́р</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">amúr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амур.html>аму́ра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амур.html>аму́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амур.html>аму́ров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cupid <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">representation of the god Cupid as a boy with a bow and arrow</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> handsome boy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">plural only<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> love affairs</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:амур.html>аму́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Amúr</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Amur river</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***анализ.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:анализ.html>ана́лиз</a> (2692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анализ.html>ана́лиз</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">análiz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анализ.html>ана́лиза</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анализ.html>ана́лизы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:анализ.html>ана́лизов</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аналитический.html>аналити́ческий</a> (12078)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">анали́т(ика)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">analít(ika)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аналитический.html>аналити́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">analitíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>analytic</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***аналог.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аналог.html>ана́лог</a> (11905)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аналог.html>ана́лог</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">análog</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аналог.html>ана́лога</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аналог.html>ана́логи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аналог.html>ана́логов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>analogue</li></ol>
